<prince-dari> How It Works
<prince-dari> see Prefs -> Smileys (main client or widget manager):
<prince-dari> Width: The width of the smiley when shown.
<prince-dari> Height: The height of the smiley when shown.
<prince-dari> Base URL: The common first part for all icons in the URL column.
<prince-dari> Code: Mibbit searches for the code of each line of text for this, and replaces it with the picture hosted on the Icon URL.
<prince-dari> URL: The second part of the URL to an image that will replace the text found in Code (or a file name if server/path is common for all icons).
